▲ Guomin News Agency, Paris, 8th - Today, the wife of Gou, the assassin of the French President, was not charged as an accomplice but temporarily detained as an important witness in the case. According to her statement during the official interrogation today, she was married in Paris last year and had a dowry of 40,000 francs. Her husband had recently abandoned all political ambitions and devoted himself to his profession, burying himself in writing books. However, according to semi-official sources, the police suspect that Gou's wife's explanation of the source of Gou's current cash and bank deposits is an excuse and that it must have been provided by a foreign political organization.

▲ Guomin News Agency, Paris, 9th - Today, officials continued to interrogate Gou's wife. According to her statement, Gou claimed that he had used his wife's dowry of 40,000 francs, and he had been very short of money recently. It is expected that this was also one of the reasons that prompted him to decide to commit the assassination. After the interrogation, Gou's wife was released, but she is not allowed to leave Paris during the period of the dowry case.

▲ Reuters, Moscow, 8th - After the assassination of French President Doumer, the Ministry of Internal Affairs issued a message stating that the murderer, Russian Gou, was a member of the Communist Party. Russian newspapers are therefore extremely angry. Russian newspapers instead accused Gou of being a White Russian and said that the French government had always protected White Russians and that Doumer's assassination was the result of this policy. The official newspaper of the Soviet Union claimed that the French strongly claimed that Gou was a member of the Communist Party and fabricated facts, which undoubtedly contained political undertones, hoping to stir up public sentiment and enable the right-wing party to win in this general election. The Communist Party's newspaper claimed that the masterminds behind Doumer's assassination were not in Russia but in Paris.

▲ Havas, Brussels, 8th - (The Belgian newspaper "L'Indépendance Belge") recently learned from its correspondent in the Czech capital about the following information about the murderer Gou: (Gou was not unknown among the Russian expatriates in Prague. After the war, he disappeared. One thing that can be determined is that Gou's name was not in the list of White Russian soldiers under General Langshell who opposed the Reds. Ten years ago, he appeared in Romania again. Soon the Soviet government allowed him to return to Russia quickly and received a Moscow passport. He immediately pretended to leave, but a few days later, it was rumored that Gou was executed after returning to Russia. "L'Indépendance Belge" also learned from another source that Gou had studied tropical medicine in Brussels, Belgium, in order to act as a Soviet Russian envoy to the Belgian Congo.)

▲ Guomin News Agency, Paris, 9th - Dimitri, a White Russian exile, committed suicide today by jumping from the sixth-floor window of his apartment. Kuomintang Central Party Headquarters 88

Holds May 9th Commemoration ▲Wang Jingwei Presents Two Important Reports ▲Establishment of Public Opinion Organs during the Tutelage Period ▲The Course of Signing the Shanghai Ceasefire Agreement

The Kuomintang Central Party Headquarters' office in Nanjing held a May 9th National Humiliation Commemoration Meeting at 9:00 AM. More than 600 people attended, including Wang Zhaoming, Shao Yuanchong, Shi Qingyang, Chen Lifu, Zhou Qigang, Chen Bijun, Fang Juehui, Shi Ying, Miao Peicheng, Li Zonghuang, Deng Feihuang, Yang Hu, Chen Fumu, Hong Ludong, Zeng Kuoqing, Zhou Zuomin, Xiao Jishan, and Gu Zhenggang.

I have been entrusted by the Central Committee to report two matters to you comrades: (1) the issue of establishing a central public opinion organ during the period of political tutelage; (2) the course of signing the Shanghai Ceasefire Agreement. Regarding the first item, the Central Political Council has held two formal meetings and two discussion meetings, conducting detailed discussions. Although a complete decision has not yet been made, firstly, everyone agrees that a central public opinion organ should be established; secondly, the majority opinion favors using the name 'National Political Participation Council' rather than 'National Assembly'; thirdly, after the central public opinion organ is established, elected legislative and supervisory members should be dismissed to avoid duplication. Everyone should know that this is an important task to complete political tutelage and achieve constitutional government and should pay close attention to it.

Regarding the second item, the full text of the agreement has been published in various newspapers, and the Minister of Foreign Affairs has also issued a statement, which everyone must have seen. In summary, there are about three points I can tell you: (1) this agreement is entirely for a ceasefire and troop withdrawal and has no political nature; (2) the Northeast issue will not cease negotiations because of this; (3) the Chinese side has sent police to take over the lost territories. Everyone must know that diplomacy depends on military strength, military strength depends on economic, cultural, and all scientific equipment, and all of these depend on politics. Politics is the foundation of everything. In the future, we will continue to maintain a policy of negotiating on one hand and resisting on the other," etc.

Wuhan Plans for Flood Prevention 92

▲Continuous Rain and Rising Yangtze River Water Level ▲Wutai Sluice Gate is Dangerous and Rescue is Being Prepared

Hankou Correspondence: The floods in Hubei Province last year were most severe in Wuhan. The prosperous markets were completely turned into swamps, and the number of people affected by the disaster was more than 770,000, with property losses of tens of millions. People from all walks of life, looking back on that time, never fail to talk about the flood with pale faces. An investigation into the causes of the flood reveals about several points: (1) continuous heavy rain for ten days, sharply increasing the amount of water, and the rivers could not accommodate it; (2) the Yangtze River was blocked, and the huge amount of water could not flow smoothly; (3) the levees were not strong; (4) the rescue was not effective. Although the authorities traced the source after the incident, trying to find a once-and-for-all solution, such as suggesting dredging the Yangtze River, planning to consolidate the levees, and planning to build a flood-proof road around the city, etc., it was ultimately hindered by the situation in Fujian. It was decided that Li commanding officers Huang Renhuan and Huang Yanzhen would take two divisions and hurry into Fujian. According to the intelligence obtained by the provincial government, after the two divisions of Huang Renhuan and Huang Yanzhen recovered Yongding, they advanced towards Longyan. Now they have arrived at Dachih and Xiaochih. The Red Bandits in Zhangzhou are in a state of emergency and have transferred all the troops of Mao Zedong, the fake first army, and Huang Zhongyue, the fake 15th army, to Nan Jing to cooperate with Peng Dehuai's fake fifth army, hoping to resist stubbornly. The outposts of the two sides started contact on the 1st of this month. Currently, there are only more than 1,000 local Red Bandits in Zhangzhou City, specializing in distributing rice and collecting money to supply the front line. Generally speaking, if the Red Bandits lose in Longyan, Zhangzhou will be abandoned. As for the Red Bandits, the fake 8th Army under Luo Binghui, in the west of Fujian, took advantage of the tense situation in southern Fujian to unite with local bandits and approached Jianning, Qingliu, and Guihua. Currently, Lu Xingbang's division is guarding Guihua and Qingliu, and Zhou Zhiqun's brigade is guarding Jianning, strictly preventing Luo's bandits from fleeing in. Liu Heding's division concentrated the two brigades of Gui Zhenyuan and Jiang Yan in Shunchang Jiang Le, as a rear response. Yesterday, the chief of staff of the division headquarters, Wang Jicheng, came to the province to report the deployment in northern Fujian to Fang Shengtao. It is reported that in addition to sending Chen Weiyuan, the chief of staff of the Provincial Security Department, to Quanzhou, to discuss the deployment of southern Fujian with Chen Guohui, the brigade commander of the First Brigade of the Provincial Defense Army, and Han Huirong, the chief of staff of the 49th Division, Fang Shengtao himself plans to go to Quanzhou for inspection within a few days. However, according to today's newspaper, Xu Kexiang's division of Zhu Shaoliang's 6th Route Army, which was ordered to aid Fujian, has already been spent and the decision was not implemented.

Time passes quickly, and a year has passed. The blockage of the river remains the same, the damage to the levees remains the same, the market has not recovered at all, and many victims have not been resettled. However, in recent days, continuous heavy rain has caused the river to gradually rise, and the Wutai Sluice Gate in Wuchang has been presenting a dangerous situation. The citizens, having suffered greatly, are all deeply worried about this. The Water Conservancy Bureau is also very concerned about this. In addition to preparing for rescue, it is also planning this year's flood prevention plan and submitting it to the provincial government for review and approval. The original submission is recorded as follows:

(Within the Wuhan urban area, the flood prevention projects, except for the entire Hankou and Zihu levee in Wuchang, which have been undertaken by the Hubei Flood Relief Rehabilitation Committee, other places have those that should be repaired in advance, and those that should be protected at any time. However, the rise and fall of the water are unpredictable, and the highest water level this year cannot be predicted. Now, if the basic flood prevention projects cannot be completed entirely, and the flood prevention matters are planned in advance, it will inevitably be a temporary panic, and it is difficult to guarantee safety. If the bureau is solely responsible, then the bureau's responsibility is to manage the water conservancy of the entire province, and it cannot focus all its efforts on the corner of Wuhan. If the chambers of commerce or public works institutions of the three towns are responsible, then flood prevention is tied to the safety of Wuhan, and this matter is of great importance. It is still not thorough to handle it by only a few agencies. After careful consideration, if this year's water level rises to 47 feet on the Jianghan Customs water gauge, it is planned to organize the Wuhan Temporary Flood Prevention Committee by the following agencies and groups, in accordance with the temporary organization of the levee repair and flood prevention committee of the Construction Department last year, so that we can cooperate with each other and not be hasty. The proposed method is as follows: (1) The Wuhan Temporary Flood Prevention Committee is composed of the Hubei Construction Department, the Hubei Water Conservancy Bureau, the Hankou Municipal Government, the Hankou Public Security Bureau, the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau, the Hubei Dike Construction Fund Management Committee, six agencies, and the three chambers of commerce of Hankou, Wuchang, and Hanyang, each sending personnel to organize it, and its chairman and members will be temporarily appointed. (2) Under the committee, there are three offices: General Affairs, Accounting, and Engineering. The General Affairs Office is undertaken by the Hankou Public Security Bureau, the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau, and the Wuyang Han three chambers of commerce, handling documents, procurement, communication, transportation, and recruitment. The Accounting Office is undertaken by the Hubei Levee Construction Fund Management Committee, handling cashiers and accounting. The Engineering Office is undertaken by the Hubei Construction Department, the Water Conservancy Bureau, and the Hankou Municipal Government, handling engineering matters. In addition to the aforementioned project plans and estimates for repairs and protections, which will be submitted by the bureau in a special case, if the water level of this year's Wuhan flood prevention affairs rises to 47 feet on the Jianghan Customs water gauge, it is proposed to organize the Wuhan Temporary Flood Prevention Committee to be responsible for handling the reasons, whether it is appropriate, and it is appropriate to submit a document to your government for verification and compliance) (May 7th)

Changshu After the Ceasefire 93

Since the Shanghai Incident, various groups have been organized in this county, such as the Civilian Rescue Team and the Local Maintenance Association, which were quite excited. Now that the Shanghai Ceasefire Agreement has been signed by both sides, the groups have begun to prepare to end everything. The details are recorded as follows:

▲Refugees Will Be Sent Back to Their Hometowns

The local Red Cross Society sent relief teams to Taicang, Luduqiao, Yanglinkou and other places at the beginning of the war to rescue refugees. More than a thousand people were rescued, mostly women and children. After arriving in Changshu, the society set up the first and second reception centers to accommodate them. The issue of supplies was donated by the local enthusiasts to the association, which has been more than two months. Now that the ceasefire agreement has been signed, the refugees want to return home and have asked the directors to find ways to send them back to their hometowns. Yesterday, the reporter met with Yu Jiusi, the director of the association, who said that although the ceasefire agreement has been signed, the Japanese army on the front line has not been removed, and there are concerns that there may be further complications when the refugees return. It is now planned to send an investigation team of Cai Wenqiao and others to conduct a proper reconnaissance before sending them back to their hometowns separately.

▲Local Maintenance Association Issues Commemorative Medals

After the Fifth Army resisted the enemy at Miaohang, it was ordered to come to Changshu for recuperation. At that time, the 47th, 87th, and 88th divisions arrived in Changshu and were stationed there. For the convenience of all parties to make contact, the county government convened various agencies, groups, and local gentry to organize a local maintenance committee, with the county magistrate, the head of the public security bureau, the president of the chamber of commerce, and the party committee member taking turns to serve as executive officers, specializing in contacting the army, dealing with ships, stationed locations, and procurement, etc. All the clerks are working around the clock. Now that the end of the work is approaching, the association has made various commemorative medals for the officers, all of whom are volunteers, and will be distributed at the end of the work as a souvenir. As for the expenses of the association, including the construction of the former office, etc., it is about more than 100,000 yuan.

▲Civilian Rescue Team is About to Return to Changshu

When the front-line war broke out, the general young patriots of this county, in view of the fact that our army bravely killed the enemy, but occasionally were injured and lacked treatment, there was the organization of the civilian rescue team, with more than 40 participants. Later, some of them went to Taicang in order to work on the ground. At that time, the 19th Route Army stationed there was short of such talents and was very welcomed, and was ordered to be incorporated into the team under the command of the 156th Brigade. When there was a small contact at the front, the team followed the army to perform rescue work. Now that the major event is roughly over, the volunteer army of various routes has been ordered to return, and the Civilian Rescue Team has also been ordered by the 19th Route Army to return to Changshu immediately. It is heard that the people in this question will open a welcome meeting when the team returns to Changshu to praise the team for its national efforts, and ask to report the situation on the front line.

▲Special Rescue Team Will Return to Shanghai

The Shanghai Red Cross Society organized a rescue team, with as many as 22 teams, after the January 28 Incident occurred. Later, after our army retreated to the second line of defense, the association merged the 22 teams into a special rescue team, with 80 to 90 team members, and appointed Zhang Zhenyan as the captain to go to Suzhou to prepare for work. Later, I don’t know why the entire team was transferred to Changshu and stationed in the Qu's ancestral hall in Zhucaobang. Captain Zhang soon went to Yixing, and the front line was also quite quiet, and there was nothing to do. Now it is also in the process of sorting out and will soon return to Shanghai.

Wuxi 95

▲Impersonating a Reporter to Collect Money Exposed

Shao Bofang, the owner of Zhao Tang Coal Yard Nongkou Tianbao Inn, was arrested by Li Xiongbiiao, the Fifth Team of the Railway Artillery Team of the Land, Sea and Air Force at 2 pm on the 1st of this month. It is heard that the reason for his arrest was actually due to the owner of a certain number in that place purchasing military hemp bags by mistake. Shao's wife, Yang, was very anxious after learning about it. At that time, Chu Boqin, a native of Liyang, impersonated a reporter from Mingbao Newspaper and claimed to Shao Yang that this matter was very small and that he could find a way to bail him out, so there was no need to worry, but he needed 200 yuan. At the same time, Tang Shuji, the owner of De Tai Tin Foil Shop in Jiangyin Lane, and Hua Fengshan, the owner of Rifengyuan Noodle Restaurant in Coal Yard Lane, also said that Chu Boqin could be asked to find a way. Shao Yang believed it when she heard the words, so she borrowed 200 yuan from the Huzhentai Rice Shop in Fangxi and agreed with Shao's friend Zhang Wenxuan and Duan Youjian to hand over the money to Chu et al. at the Minsheng Building Teahouse near the station and explained that in addition to the 200 yuan, they would need to send an additional reward of 100 yuan and Chu Boqin 50 yuan, limited to noon that day. After the agreement was reached, Chu immediately took the money to the Yuejia car, not knowing what kind of hookup he was doing. Half an hour later, Li ordered Shao Yang to find three guarantors to bail Shao Bofang home. By the next day, Chu went to Shao's house to thank Shao, Shao refused sternly because the circumstances were suspicious. It lasted for three days and still could not be formally resolved. The matter was detected by Qin Hongye, the backbone of Mingbao Newspaper, and because it was related to the reputation of all newspaper reporters and this newspaper, he reported to the fifth branch of the Public Security Bureau for investigation at 8 am the day before. Director Peng arrested Chu Boqin according to the report and summoned the principal Shao Yang to the bureau, transferred it to the head office, and forwarded it to the prosecutor's office of the county court. After the prosecutor Du opened the court, he ordered Shao Yang to send him back, Chu Boqin was detained and awaited trial.

Jiangyin 96

▲Road Association Investigates Fraud

The Jiangsu Provincial Road Promotion Branch has been established for five days in the Zhaozong Ancestral Hall on Zhong Street. The association discovered that He Shipan, the chief executive, had used the name of the association to go to Rixin Tuo to privately print the sea gate mu donation receipt book and forge documents in an attempt to defraud money. The executive director meeting decided to send He to the county government for questioning and went to Rixin Studio to find the evidence. Magistrate Ma questioned him at night and ordered him to be imprisoned and await trial.

Qingjiang 97

▲Execution of Police Captain for Colluding with Bandits

Liu Zhongzhi, the captain of the third squad of the Huaiyin County Police, was originally the company commander under Ma Yuren during the warlord era and was in secret communication with bandits in various counties in Huai, supplying the bandits with guns and ammunition. After Ma's failure, he went elsewhere for a while. In the 19th year of the Republic of China, he was filled with his current position due to the reputation of a certain director in Huaiyin, and was assigned to Songji and other places in this county. He recruited bandit leaders Ding Zhaohuai, Zheng Xuewu, Wu Xingfang, etc. as disciples, privately lent the public and private guns under his control to bandits to rob people, and harbored hostages and demanded fields. There were many accumulated cases, and the villagers were afraid of his power and dared to be angry but did not dare to speak out. A month ago, the Wang Yanshen Brigade of Liang Guanying's 25th Route Army was ordered to suppress the bandits in various counties in Jiangbei. After detecting Liu's bad deeds and hearing that bandit leaders Ding Zhaohuai and others were hiding in his house, he immediately sent a team to Liu's residence in Dupaifang to search and arrest them. Ding and others had already fled upon hearing the news. Liu was arrested, submitted to the headquarters for questioning and found to be true, and was immediately sentenced to death according to law. At 11 am today (3rd), Liu was brought to court for identification, tied up and taken to the Qingyang small railway station, and executed by shooting.

Wuhu 98

▲Beijing-Wuhu Liner Robbed Midway

The small liners operating on the Yangtze River in Wuhu have been repeatedly robbed by bandits, and there is no good way to prevent it. Merchants and travelers regard it as a dangerous place. Yesterday, the Wu Ning Liner of the Nanjing-Wuhu class Xifeng Company sailed from Beijing to Wuhu, carrying many passengers. At one hour and three quarters in the morning, when it was near Heshanggang downstream of Caishi, four bandits suddenly appeared, with three pistols and a broadsword in total. Two people jumped into the old big house and ordered them to turn around and open downstream. They immediately began to search, back and forth as many as seven or eight times. No one on the entire ship was spared. There was a certain head of the Dangtu Wounded Soldiers Hospital who received 2,500 yuan in supplies and a box cannon in Beijing, and the travel expenses of hundreds of female students from Wuwei Visiting Group and more than 700 liang of raw opium of a certain soil dealer were all searched. There was also an old woman who was shot in the breast and died on the spot while arguing with the robbers for three silver coins. The small liner was forced to spin in the river, and viewers on both sides were blocking the river. Two hours later, they carried the stolen goods onto a rowboat and escaped. At that time, one of the robbers wearing a suit accidentally fired his box cannon when getting off the rowboat because he was carrying too many stolen goods, injuring his leg. After the bandits boarded the boat and left the wheel, the self-defense groups of Dangtu and He County opened fire on both sides to pursue them. Until 9 pm, the small liner arrived in Wuhu, and the estimated loss was more than 10,000 yuan.

Northeastern Volunteer Army Support Association 99

Held Yesterday's Temporary Standing Committee Meeting ▲Passed the Detailed Rules of the Fundraising Committee ▲Wu Zhaogang's Department Came to Report the Conclusion of the Day

The Northeastern Volunteer Army Support Association held its fifth temporary standing council meeting at Jing'an Villa at 10:00 am yesterday. Li Cishan was elected chairman, and it was discussed that a general meeting of members would be held at 3:00 pm this Wednesday (tomorrow) at No. 89 Ren'an Lane, Guling Road, and a board meeting would be held at the same location at 5:00 pm to discuss further matters. The full text of the detailed rules of the fundraising committee was also passed yesterday, and excerpts are as follows:

(1) The fundraising committee is organized in accordance with the provisions of Article 10 of the organizational outline of the Northeastern Volunteer Army Support Association. (2) The fundraising committee shall elect several permanent members to handle daily affairs. (3) All directors of this association may attend the meetings of the fundraising committee. (4) If the fundraising committee believes that there should be fundraising committee members or other positions to be appointed, it may suggest that the standing council review and appoint them. (5) The fundraising committee should carry out the tasks of raising military funds and collecting military supplies. (6) The fundraising methods of the fundraising committee shall be freely determined by the fundraising committee, and those of important relations shall be approved by the council. (7) The receipts for fundraising of the fundraising committee shall be prepared by the standing council for use. (8) The fundraising committee shall meet at least once a week. (9) The donations directly received by the fundraising committee shall be sent to the bank designated by the association in real time and deposited into the association's savings account for relief, and the standing council and the custody committee shall be notified in writing for verification. Those who do not directly receive the funds shall report the names and donations of the agreed donors to the two associations for assessment. (10) When the fundraising committee needs a secretary, it shall be decided by the standing council meeting. (11) If it is necessary to amend these regulations, it shall be decided by the council meeting.

Wu Zhaogang's department of the 10th Route Army of the Liaoning Volunteer Army has more than 20,000 people, with complete guns and horses. Since the Shenyang Incident, it has repeatedly fought fiercely with Japan, such as the Jinxi Xingcheng Xinmin Liuhegou and other battles, and has won considerable victories. It is now heard that the department wants the compatriots in the south to understand the recent situation in the Northeast, and has specially sent Xu Jinyai, the political minister of the department, Xiao Ruipeng, the investigation section chief of the political department, Li Xinming, the secretary-general, Wu Zhidong and Yang Shijie, the adjutant office, and Liu Xinyuan, the communicator, etc. to Shanghai to report on the anti-Japanese experience and ask for assistance from all walks of life.

19th Route Army Has No Air Force Organization 101

Regarding the matter of the 19th Route Army organizing an air force, which was published in yesterday's Chinese and foreign newspapers, this reporter went to the rear office of the 19th Route Army to inquire. According to the responsible staff there, the air force is a part of the national defense forces and must have an overall plan. It must also be planned in its entirety by the central government. No military force can act on its own. The 19th Route Army has absolutely no plan for this matter. As for the overseas Chinese in various ports, although some wanted to help this army with airplanes during the Sino-Japanese war, this army had no airfield at that time and lacked the necessary equipment. Overseas Chinese were separately notified by telegram to send the donations to the central government for reception. The current situation is not known in detail, but the so-called reception of airplanes donated by overseas Chinese is not factual. As for Zhang Huichang's visit to Shanghai, although he met with Chiang Kai-shek and Cai Tingkai, they never discussed the organization of an air force. It is ridiculous that the Chinese and foreign newspapers are widely reporting that the 19th Route Army appointed Zhang Huichang, Ding Ji, and Xu as the commander and deputy commanders of the air force, respectively. Commercial Shipping Carrying Overseas Chinese Students in Japan to Return Home Suspended 103

When the Sino-Japanese situation was urgent, the Ministry of Transportation ordered the Shanghai Maritime Affairs Bureau to consult with the Shipping Association and the Da Lai Company. The company's ships would carry poor overseas Chinese students back to the country each time they passed through Japan. It was agreed that the fare for those boarding in Yokohama would be reduced to 27 yuan per person, and 23 yuan for those boarding in Kobe. It was scheduled to be implemented immediately. However, according to the Maritime Affairs Bureau yesterday, since the armistice agreement has been signed, commerce can gradually recover. Therefore, the Da Lai ship's plan to carry overseas Chinese students back to the country has been suspended.

Li Mingzhong and Jiang Mingji Executed by Firing Squad 105

▲Zhang Mingyuan Sentenced to Life Imprisonment ▲Zhou Gan臣 and Others Released

Li Mingzhong and eleven others, the initiators of the Southeast Self-Defense Army, were secretly reported to the Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau. Director Wen dispatched detectives to cooperate with concession detectives to arrest more than ten people separately at the Dadong Hotel and other places. After being interrogated by the Judicial Section of the bureau, they were sent to the Songhu Garrison Headquarters. After further detailed questioning by Wang Yi, the Chief of the Military Law Department of the headquarters, Li and the other eleven people, as well as the case files and evidence, were transferred to the Military and Political Department of Nanjing. After separate interrogations by Wang Zhennan, the Chief of the Military Law Division, Li Mingzhong, Jiang Mingji, and Zhang Mingyuan confessed that there was sufficient evidence of internal strife. They were sent to the Second Isolation Room of the prison department of the department in Sanyuan Lane and detained. A request was submitted to Chiang Kai-shek, the Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission, for punishment. The crime committed by the suspect was endangering the Republic of China, and an order was given to execute them separately. Therefore, on the morning of May 2nd, the department brought Li Mingzhong and Jiang Mingji to the execution ground in front of the Second Isolation Room of the prison department for execution by firing squad after the execution office verified their identities. Zhang Mingyuan was sentenced to life imprisonment. The rest, Zhou Gan臣, Sun Yushu, Song Botao, Yin Yuting, etc., were all released.

Wu Tiecheng Discusses Guangdong Matters 108

Ren Luping Dies of Illness 113

▲The Coffin Will Be Sealed This Afternoon Ren Luping, the director of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau in Caojiadu, Shanghai West, died at about 1:30 PM the day before yesterday. He participated in the closing ceremony of the Kangjiaqiao War Zone Refugee Shelter. He made a speech on stage and took pictures. While talking to the guests and drinking tea, he suddenly felt dizzy and fell to the ground. The attendant police officers immediately helped him back to his residence in Minzhili, Hatong Road, but he was unconscious. Famous Chinese and Western doctors were immediately called for treatment. It was said that it was a cerebral hemorrhage, or a stroke. The treatment was ineffective, and he passed away at 8:40 PM. The coffin will be sealed today (the 10th) at 1 PM, and the funeral will be held on the afternoon of the 12th. Ren's given name is Xiechen, and he was nearly forty years old. He was from Henan and served in the police force for many years. He was honest, straightforward, and his integrity was admirable. When Dai Shifu was the director, Ren was the inspector. Because of his diligence in handling affairs, he was soon appointed as the director of the Second Branch of the Second District in Nanshi. When Director Yuan took office, Ren's achievements were even more remarkable. Before long, he was promoted to the director of the Seventh District, and finally to his current position. However, Caojiadu is a place with many factories and a large population, and the area is vast, making it difficult to manage. But Ren handled it with ease. After the January 28th Incident broke out, Ren stayed in the office for a long time, personally supervising his subordinates to maintain the local area, day and night, without the slightest slack. Later, because the 19th Route Army retreated to the Second Defense Line, the Japanese army confiscated all the guns in the Sixth District. In this critical situation, Ren was not afraid of violence and argued with reason. As a result, the Japanese army returned them in full. His courage was such. Now he has suddenly passed away, and everyone who hears about it deeply regrets it. It is said that the vacancy in the Sixth District will be filled by the current Director of the Third District, Zhang Qinming. The position in the Third District will be filled by Yu Baozhen, the assistant of the Second Section.

Record of the Municipal Federation of Associations' Representative Meeting 114

▲First Form a National Salvation Savings Preparatory Committee ▲Create a Form to Investigate the Losses of Citizens in the Special Zone

The Shanghai Special Zone Citizens' Federation of Associations held its second representative meeting yesterday afternoon at 3 PM at the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce. Each branch will send a member to prepare for the organization, and jointly solicit the participation of various public groups. (B) The term of the savings will be temporarily set for one year. (C) The depositors will send the savings directly to the designated bank, and no one may use them. It was resolved to hand it over to the executive committee for handling, and to push Chen Jicheng to create a form and send it to the various branches for distribution to the households for filling out, with a deadline for reporting. (6) Volunteer Army Issue: It was generally believed that there was no need for it to exist after the armistice agreement was signed. It was resolved that the volunteer army of the association would be disbanded immediately. (7) The association's refugee shelter closure case: It was resolved to close it within fifteen days. Those who have no home to return to will be sent to the local maintenance association, and Hu Fengxiang will be sent to negotiate first. The Social Affairs Bureau convened various groups.

Handling Contract Labor Workers 115

▲Eight Measures Resolved to Temporarily Cope with the Current Situation ▲Start an Investigation to Fundamentally Eliminate the Problem

In view of the suffering of contract labor workers, the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau specially invited various related groups yesterday afternoon at 1 PM to discuss ways to eliminate social evils and protect labor. More than twenty groups attended, including the Chinese Children's Welfare Association, the Chinese Women's Temperance Association, the War Zone Civilian Temporary Relief Association, and the Hudong Commune. More than twenty representatives attended, including Feng Liutang, Zhu Hanzhang, and Zhang Lue. The Social Affairs Bureau sent Luo Yi and Hang Dingan to attend, and Wang Zhiqin recorded the minutes. First, Chairman Luo Yi reported the purpose of the meeting, and then the issue of eliminating contract labor workers was discussed. It was resolved (1) to notify each shelter to report the number of such workers, and not to allow them to be claimed or guaranteed by the contract food providers, pending further arrangements. (2) The Social Affairs Bureau will clarify the relationship between the contract food providers and the workers to resolve disputes, and issue orders to each shelter to handle the matter in accordance with the following two measures: (A) The maintenance groups will issue certificates to the contract food providers for the original family members to inquire about the contract food providers, with evidence to rely on. (B) The maintenance groups will send letters to the family members of the workers. (3) Each shelter will notify the family members of the workers to claim them, and explain the secrets of the contract labor system. If they wish the charitable organizations to maintain or introduce them to work, they can do as they please. (4) Before the family members of the workers claim them, each children's welfare group should share the responsibility of sheltering and educating them. When they reach the legal age of child labor, which is fourteen years old, the maintenance groups should try to introduce them to work in factories. (5) When introducing the workers to work, it must be stipulated with the factory that the wages belong to the workers, or temporarily deposited in the maintenance group and transferred to the workers' family members. (6) When introducing the workers to work, it must be stipulated with the factory that the provisions of Articles 6 and 7 of the Factory Law should be followed, and there should be no discrimination or abuse. (7) The groups that introduce the workers to work should periodically check on the living conditions of the workers after they enter the factory to fulfill their responsibility of guaranteeing them. (8) Investigate the actual situation of the system in order to eliminate it thoroughly.

Cheng Yu Company

Reasons for Opposing the Installation of Main Water Meters 117

The Shui Yu Company sent a letter to the Shanghai Real Estate Association yesterday, stating: To Whom It May Concern, the water company suddenly sent workers to our company's Runyu Lane, Yangshupu Road, to install main water meters without obtaining our company's consent beforehand, nor was there any notification. This abruptness is deeply regrettable. We have checked the letter from the company to your association, which stated that in order to save water, there is a desire to install meters. Our company does not oppose this in principle, but in order to prevent waste, it is necessary to install a water meter for each household, as promised in the original letter, and to directly collect water fees from the tenants in order to be effective, in the same proportion as residents' electricity use. The owners should not bear any responsibility, but in order to be considerate of the tenants and avoid the cumbersome procedures of installing and removing water meters, the owners may pay the meter price and deposit on behalf of the tenants. If the water is measured according to the current main meter system of the company, it is equivalent to adding the cost of water wasted by the tenants to the owners, what is the meaning of saving? Our company cannot recognize this and asks your association to negotiate with the company to implement the proposal of installing meters for each household. We would be most grateful. Sincerely, Women's Christian Temperance Union Labor Department

Labor Day Commemoration Meeting Held 118

The female workers of the Labor Department paid great attention to Labor Day, so they held the third Labor Day commemoration meeting at the society on May 8th. All participants felt that female workers should bear a great mission in the future.

Miscellaneous Grain and Sesame Cake Trade Association Notice 119

The Shanghai Chinese Miscellaneous Grain and Sesame Cake Trade Association yesterday announced to the fellow trades, stating that when the Japanese occupied Shanghai, they saw a large amount of activity in Yangtze River trade, and Shanghai is a distribution area for goods, especially the source of recovery of the Yangtze River. The most important reason for the Japanese army's massacre in Shanghai during this Shanghai incident is this point. We should all uphold the responsibility of every citizen for the rise and fall of the country. At this time when national hatred has not been avenged, we should unanimously reject Japanese goods. This association adheres to this position and will not allow itself to slack off. Therefore, it was resolved at the 26th executive committee meeting yesterday that if any member of the trade privately orders goods from Japanese merchants or ships them on Japanese ships, once discovered, the association will recognize the member as a public enemy and immediately expel them from the association. The entire trade will be notified not to buy or sell, and the same will be done in the case of substitutions. This is hereby posted, hoping that all trades will understand this intention and take note. This is of utmost importance. Taxpayers Association Sends Letter to Public Works Department

Request That the Yan Yutang Kidnapping Case Be Solved Within a Time Limit 120

▲Patrol Officers Lack Training, Allowing Bandits to Escape ▲It Is Deeply Regrettable That Taxpayers Do Not Enjoy Protection

The Public Concession Chinese Taxpayers Association, based on a letter from the Jiangxi Road Business Association stating that the patrol officers did not do their best in pursuing the bandits when Yan Yutang of the Guangyu Business Company was kidnapped, which seemed to be due to a lack of training, sent a letter to the Director-General of the Public Works Department yesterday, requesting that the case be solved within a time limit. The original letter stated: To Whom It May Concern, the Jiangxi Road Business Association reported that Yan Yutang, the general manager of the Guangyu Business Company on this road, was driving his own car to the company entrance at 8:30 AM on the 4th of this month, when four or five bandits suddenly came up to the car with guns. Two bandits pointed their guns at the driver, forbidding him to make a sound, and monitored the driver. The remaining bandits monitored the victim, driving the car straight to the intersection of Jiangxi Road and Avenue Edward VII, forcing the driver out of the car, and sped away. When he was kidnapped, a Chinese constable on Jiangxi Road and Five Horse Road witnessed the situation. Only after the car left did he blow the whistle. Three or four patrol officers arrived later. The kidnapped car happened to drive to the intersection of Avenue Edward VII and Jiangxi Road. The red light stopped it for three minutes. The patrol officers only blew the whistle lightly behind it and did not pursue it, allowing it to escape and drive away. The Public Works Department is responsible for the improper maintenance of law and order, and after the incident, it did not fulfill its duties to apprehend the bandits. This is due to poor training. This matter concerns the local security and responsibilities. We should request your association to protest to the Public Works Department as soon as possible, to solve the case within a time limit, in order to maintain commerce and protect security, etc. We have received this request. The police officers must be brave and agile when dealing with bandits. According to the Jiangxi Road Business Association, there was an opportunity to rescue Yan Yutang. However, because the patrol officers of your bureau lacked training and were unable to respond to the situation in a timely manner, lacking both courage and agility, they allowed Yan to be kidnapped by the bandits, failing to provide the protection he was entitled to under his tax obligations. This is deeply regrettable. In accordance with the previous letter, we should request your bureau to investigate the case thoroughly as soon as possible, solve the case within a time limit, and order all police officers to pay close attention to it in the future in order to maintain law and order. Do not fail to do so.

Yesterday was the day of Detective Jin's funeral. The French Chief Inspector, Feiber, along with Western Detective Chief Inspectors from various police stations, and Hua Detective Chief Inspector Tao Defu, led a group of inspectors, deputy inspectors, and detectives to pay their respects at the funeral altar at noon. Shortcut for Transportation to Kunshan, Taicang, and Jiading 125

Since the railway was interrupted, transportation from Shanghai to Kunshan, Taicang, and Jiading counties has had to go through Suzhou, making transportation very inconvenient. Moreover, banditry frequently occurs, making travelers feel particularly uneasy. Now, the Qingpu Yuanjin Steamboat Bureau has specially prepared the Yuan Chang Fast Steamer, which departs from Shanghai for Zhujiajiao every day at 6:30 AM on odd days of the Gregorian calendar. It can connect with the Hongfei Steamer departing from Zhujiajiao to Kunshan and the steamboat to Anting. This route is indeed faster and safer than going through Suzhou, and passengers can travel comfortably. If passengers have inquiries or entrustment matters, they can call 40441 for inquiries. The bureau will wholeheartedly handle them.

News from Various Native Place Associations 127

▲Anhui Various Anhui native place organizations in Shanghai held a joint meeting yesterday, attended by more than 100 representatives from the Anhui, Huining, Jindou, Hehan, Taiping, Wuyuan, and Xiuning native place associations, as well as various industrial, commercial, and professional organizations, including Bai Liewu, Li Zhenya, Yu Langxi, Cao Zhigong, Hu Peiru, and Luo Chunfu. Then, they began discussing and resolving the following motions: (1) The Anhui Provincial Garrison Brigade's funding is currently the responsibility of the provincial government. A telegram should be sent to the central and provincial governments stating that the aforementioned troops should be under the command of the provincial government; otherwise, they should not be funded by the Anhui treasury. (2) A telegram should be sent to the provincial government requesting the cancellation of the budget from Chen Tiaoyuan's administration and restoring the original status quo to conserve resources. (3) A telegram should be sent to the provincial government requesting the maintenance of educational funding and making it independent. (4) Wuyuan is facing a border crisis with communist bandits, Jing County has been captured by bandits, and the Tunxi security police have mutinied. A telegram should be sent to the provincial government requesting the immediate dispatch of troops to suppress the bandits to prevent them from spreading. (5) A telegram should be sent to the central and provincial governments requesting the cancellation of the salt surcharge and eight types of special taxes on tobacco seedlings. (6) The provincial government should be requested to organize a committee to investigate the financial chaos of past years. At least two-thirds of the members of this committee must be representatives of public organizations. (7) A telegram should be sent to the provincial government urgently requesting assistance to the people in self-defense and preparing for genuine local autonomy. (8) A telegram should be sent to the central government requesting an investigation into those involved in corruption in Anhui's disaster relief efforts. (9) He Qigong, the Director of the Anhui Department of Finance, has come to Shanghai. Representatives should be sent to meet with him and inquire about the financial situation of Anhui Province. (10) A telegram should be sent to the provincial government stating that various provincial taxes must not be collected directly by the military to avoid disrupting the system. (11) The provincial government should be requested to rectify official corruption and clarify corruption. (12) Xia Zhiqin, Xu Bolong, Li Zhenya, Cao Zhigong, Hu Peiru, and others were elected to draft a proposal to be submitted to the provincial government to improve provincial administration. The meeting adjourned after the discussion. ▲Fenghua The Fenghua Native Place Association in Shanghai held an executive committee meeting yesterday, attended by more than 20 people, including Chen Zhonggao. Chen Zhonggao was publicly elected as the chairman. (B) Regarding a letter from Standing Committee member Kang Nian, stating that a fellow villager's orphan, Wang Chaosui, is working at the Shanghai Weiyi Woolen Mill and requesting a letter to be sent to temporarily take him back to his hometown for reunion, a letter will be prepared to the factory to collect him. (C) Regarding a letter from member Ma Houfu, stating that his home in the countryside has been defiled, which is detrimental to hygiene, and requesting a letter to be sent to the village chief of his village to prohibit and control the situation, a letter will be sent to the village chief for nearby mediation. The above factual details were submitted for retroactive approval and were approved by the members. It was decided to contact the Ningbo Native Place Association in Shanghai for handling. (3) Regarding the letter from the Shanghai Municipal Rent Reduction Movement Committee regarding donations from various organizations, it was submitted for discussion and was decided to approve the donation. (4) A written opinion on the organization of village defense groups was proposed by Standing Committee member Wang Shijia. Congestion at Post Office Remittance 129

Tailor Swindles Old Woman's Money ▲Clerk Provides Proof ▲Lu Jinzhang to be Sentenced Shu Xushi, an old woman from Wuwei County, Anhui Province, works as a helper at No. 10 Yongchang Lane, Xiaobang Bay, French Concession. The day before yesterday at noon, she took seven silver dollars to the Baxianqiao Post Office to remit home for use. At the time, the post office was crowded with people remitting money, and she could not get to the counter. Lu Jinzhang, a tailor from Yangzhou who lives at No. 7 Ma'an Lane, Chongqing Road, was also there to remit silver dollars home. Seeing that she could not get to the counter, he pretended to be well-intentioned and offered to hand the silver dollars over for her. She believed him to be true and handed the silver dollars over to the counter. Unexpectedly, Lu had malicious intentions and wanted to seize the money. He wrote his own Yangzhong County address on the remittance slip to retrieve the receipt and escape. She discovered his deception, grabbed him, and demanded the receipt. During the argument, a clerk with the surname Lü confirmed that Lu had unlawful intentions and immediately called the police to send the person and evidence to the police station. Yesterday, he was sent to Criminal Division 1 of the Second Special District Court. Fei Xizhen, the police station's lawyer, explained the case, stating that the case was clear. If the plaintiff entrusted the defendant to hand over the money, then the defendant committed the crime of embezzlement. If the defendant conspired to hand over the money, it was considered embezzlement and should be handled according to the law. The plaintiff then stated the previous events. A postal worker with the surname Lü also testified in court, proving the defendant's unlawful actions. When questioned, the defendant Lu Jinzhang continued to deny the charges and refused to admit guilt. Presiding Judge Wu Fanglian stated that the case was clear and that no denial would be allowed. He then announced the conclusion of the debate and scheduled a date for sentencing. The defendant was returned to custody. The remittance slip with the evidence was sent to the police station to be returned to the postal worker with instructions to correct the address and send it. Hujiamuqiao.

Lu Qingcai, also known as Lu San, from Jiangbei, was arrested last September by his accomplice Chen Sanwenzijing of the Chief Patrol Room, who confessed to participating in kidnapping activities. Chinese and Western detectives then brought Chen, the thief, to the French Concession to arrest Lu. During the investigation, Lu suddenly fell ill and was returned to the hospital by the police station. He died in the hospital within a few days. After examination by the court, his wife, Lu Yinshi, was ordered to collect the body. Unexpectedly, she hired a lawyer to file a criminal self-accusation with the First Special District Local Court, accusing Zhou Honglin, the detective in charge of the case at the Chief Inspection Office, of demanding a bribe of 2,000 yuan from her husband, Lu Qingcai. When the time came for repayment, not only did he not return the money, but he also falsely accused her husband of being a kidnapper, and arrested him and abused him with torture, causing Lu's death. She requested that he be convicted of murder for money and that the loan be recovered. The case has been repeatedly opened and investigated. The previous newspaper reported repeatedly about this case. Yesterday was the date of sentencing. Trial of Drunk Man Who Killed His Wife Begins 132

▲Peacemaker Killed ▲Wait for Family to Arrive Before Questioning Ding Xingzi, a man from Yangzhou, came to Shanghai from Hankou earlier. He learned that his wife, Mao Guiying, from Hubei Province, had developed a relationship with a certain adjutant surnamed Chen and was unwilling to follow him as a wife. In a moment of anger, at noon on the 3rd of this month, he took a knife while drunk to No. 195 Dongyouheng Road, in the pavilion room upstairs of his home, and stabbed Guiying in the forehead and other parts of her body. Her mother, Mao Gao, and aunt, Gao Xushi, intervened to mediate, but were also stabbed to the ground by Ding. They were all sent to the Tongren Hospital for treatment. As a result, Gao Xushi died of her injuries. The Hongkou police station heard the alarm and dispatched Chinese detective Liu Zhaonian to take Ding Xingzi, along with two murder weapons, to the First Special District Court. The details of the interrogation and the examination of Gao Xushi have been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Shen Bingrong presided over a continued interrogation at the First Court. Zhang Tianyin, the police lawyer, stated that the victims, Mao Guiying and Mao Gao, had slightly recovered from their injuries and were in court to testify. When questioned, Mao Guiying testified that she was 19 years old and the defendant was her husband. Last October, her aunt, Gao Xushi (the deceased), acted as matchmaker and she married Ding in Shanghai at the Yuegong Hotel on Sichuan Road. However, she previously had a husband with a certain surname and had long been divorced. During the previous Shanghai war, she and her mother and sister took refuge in the Guangtailai Inn on Avenue Edward VII in the French Concession. At that time, the defendant was still at home taking care of the house. Because his mother and former wife both ran brothels in Hankou, and his wife was also a prostitute, her mother (Mao Gao) had instructed him to go to Hankou and bring his mother and wife to Shanghai. Unexpectedly, he returned to Shanghai the other day, only bringing his son, Xiao Mao (4 years old), and three prostitutes, Lao San and Azhu. At the Guangtailai Inn, she was questioned by her mother, and her aunt, Gao Xushi (the deceased), also scolded him for being willing to live as a cuckold and not bringing his mother and wife to Shanghai. She then planned to temporarily live in a church for a month, and the defendant harbored resentment. The next day, they returned to their home at No. 195 Dongyouheng Road for lunch. He drank a cup of Shaoxing wine. After a while, after the meal was over, he secretly locked the door and produced two sharp knives, one from her home and one he had hidden beforehand, and stabbed her in the forehead, then stabbed her in the hand. At that time, her mother (Mao Gao) quickly pulled him away, and her aunt, Gao Xushi, also stepped forward to persuade him, but they were all stabbed and fell to the ground. The defendant accused her of having an affair with a certain adjutant, which was not true. Her mother, Mao Gao, stated that Guiying was her biological daughter. Last autumn, her daughter went to visit her aunt, Gao Xushi. He saw her and immediately asked her to act as matchmaker and married her at the Yuegong Hotel in Shanghai. Later, they went to Hankou and learned that he had a wife who was a prostitute, so they quarreled and returned to Shanghai. They rented a house on the same road. Earlier, because she had instructed him to go to Hankou and feared that his mother and wife would come to Shanghai, he only brought his son and two young prostitutes. She slightly condemned him, and he developed this vicious intention, leading to this tragedy. She was stabbed in the waist and hand in two places. The family of the deceased (Gao Xushi) will come to Shanghai in a few days. When questioned, the defendant stated that because his wife wanted to go to the church, he was momentarily upset, and because he was drunk, he intended to intimidate his wife Guiying with a knife and did not intend to kill her. The injuries to Mao Gao and the deceased Gao Xushi were due to drunkenness and confusion, and he stabbed them involuntarily. He asked for leniency. Judge Shen ordered him to remain in custody and wait for the family of the deceased to arrive before questioning. Mao Guiying and Mao Gao were taken by the court clerk to the forensic room to examine the injuries.

Forging Checks to Obtain 2,000 Taels of Silver 133

▲Sentenced to One Year and Six Months of Imprisonment Zhuo Qingen, a 26-year-old Cantonese, was an employee in the current account department of the Hong Kong National Savings Bank on Jiangxi Road. On April 22nd, he used fraudulent means to forge a check and impersonate the seal of depositor Hong Li to withdraw 2,000 taels of silver from the Women's Commercial Savings Bank on Nanjing Road and deposit it privately into the Shanghai Bank. The National Bank discovered the incident and reported it to the Chief Patrol Room the day before yesterday. Chinese and Western detectives were dispatched to arrest Zhuo and seize 400 silver dollars and a deposit slip from the Shanghai Bank with a balance of 100 yuan. He was taken to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, he was sent to Criminal Division 1 of the First Special District Court. Qian Xunjiu, the police lawyer, stated the case and said that the money deposited in the Shanghai Bank by the defendant had been gradually withdrawn. In addition to the 400 yuan seized from the defendant, only 100 yuan remained on the deposit slip. Zheng Jiaju, an employee in the accounting department of the National Bank, also filed a case, explaining everything. When questioned, the defendant said that he did not know who put the check in his drawer, and the seal had already been affixed. It was true that he sent his brother-in-law Liang Zhenpeng to collect it. After verifying the confession, Judge Qian Hongye sentenced the defendant Zhuo Qingen to one year and six months of imprisonment for using forged valuable vouchers to fraudulently obtain property, and imposed a fine of 500 yuan. If the fine is not paid in full, it will be converted into imprisonment at a rate of two yuan per day. The forged check will be confiscated. In the accompanying civil lawsuit, the defendant should compensate the plaintiff with 2,000 taels of silver and statutory interest from April 22nd of this year until the date of the end of the execution. The 400 silver dollars and the remaining balance of 100 yuan deposited in the Shanghai Commercial Savings Bank Yaoji account are allowed to be seized.

Dr. Cen Provides Free Medical Care to the Poor and Sick 136

Dr. Cen Zhongming, a traditional Chinese medicine practitioner at No. 504 Dexing Lane, Haining Road, has been practicing medicine in Shanghai for more than ten years. All those who suffer from illness and receive his treatment are revived, and he has saved countless lives every year. Last year, when the Japanese entered Guanzhabei, refugees fled to the concessions, and some of them were ill. Dr. Cen felt compassion for them and provided free consultations at the Asia Hotel on Avenue Edward VII and at the Tianji Hall on Wuma Road, not taking any fees. Therefore, many refugees suffering from illness received his treatment. Now that the situation has calmed down, Cen has returned to his residence to practice medicine as usual, but he continues to provide free consultations to the poor and sick.

Customs Broker Involved in Red Pill Trafficking Case 142

▲Tried Yesterday by the Second Special Court Ying Xiyuan, from Hangzhou, the owner of the Dashun Transportation Company behind the South Railway Station, was previously investigated and seized by detectives from the 2nd District Public Security Bureau for smuggling the poisonous substance red pills. Ying and the stolen goods were taken to the bureau for interrogation. According to his confession, Yu Xin'gong Customs Brokerage, located at No. 5 Jilifang, Diandang Street, French Concession, entrusted him to transport them. The bureau requested the French Concession Police to send detectives to Yu Xin'gong to arrest the owner, Li Yushan, who was not present. Only Zhang Pekui, a partner, and Li Zhushi, the wife of the owner, were found. Ten items were seized and taken to the police station to be sent to the Second Special Court for interrogation. The Public Security Bureau sent personnel to the case, requesting the transfer. The official stated that the crime occurred in the French Concession and ordered the Public Security Bureau to send Ying and the stolen goods to the court for interrogation and verification. Zhang and Zhu were released on bail pending verification. The Public Security Bureau then sent Ying, along with the evidence, twenty small packages of red pills, two wooden boxes of medicinal powder, and two packages of white medicinal powder, to the Second Special Court for investigation. Yesterday, Zhang Pekui and Li Zhushi were summoned. Ying was sent to the court. In the afternoon, Judge Xiong Huiping presided over the trial in Criminal Division 1. First, the police lawyer Fei Xizhen stated the case. Ying Xiyuan confessed that on April 2nd, he went to Yu Xin'gong Customs Brokerage. The accountant told him that there would be two packages of stone powder to be transported to Hangzhou the next day. The next day, someone was sent to drive the truck to the company, and it was seized by the Public Security Bureau. He did not know it was red pills at the time, and there was a Yu Xin'gong note to prove it. He also hired a lawyer to defend him and requested permission to post bail. When questioned, Zhang Pekui confessed that although he wrote the note, the goods were directly entrusted to Ying for transfer by the customer Zhang Jinfu. Li Zhushi confessed that her husband, Li Yushan, had returned to his native Jiangxi, and she did not know anything about the affairs of the business. The court ordered that the trial be continued on May 16th. Ying Xiyuan was ordered to post a shop guarantee of 3,000 yuan. Zhang Pekui's guarantee was changed to 5,000 yuan. If no guarantee was provided, they would be detained. Li Zhushi was released on her original bail pending verification.

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the coastal areas of Shandong are mostly cloudy, with winds from the southwest to northwest. Correspondence 145

To whom it may concern, we, Yang Cai Hua Xian and Yang Hua Xun Yang, hereby declare that upon reading the article (Yang Shengzhi's concubine is in litigation for inheritance, and Lawyer Zhang Shizhao submitted a written opinion) published on the third page, tenth edition of Shen Bao on the 23rd of this month, it is entirely inconsistent with the facts and damages our reputation. The lawsuit filed by the late husband's concubine, Wang Jiazhen, this time was for alimony, not for inheritance. This is error one. Hua Xian and Xun Yang were both officially married by the late husband, with matchmakers, marriage certificates, and locations where the wedding ceremonies were held, all with solid evidence. Although the late husband's elder brother, Shengzhao, died in Fushun for national affairs, and he intended to marry two wives to have a son to inherit the family line, it seemed to constitute bigamy, but we were unaware of this beforehand. After negotiation, the late husband remained adamant. Now that he has passed away, how can our status be compared with Wang Jiazhen, who was redeemed from a brothel? The newspaper stated that there were three concubines, namely Cai Hua Xian and Hua Xun Yang, etc. This is error two. Hua Xian's son, Xiu Qian, is already eleven years old, and the newspaper claimed he was an eight-year-old child. This is error three. Wang Jiazhen stole clothes and valuables and fled, cohabiting with a man named Zhao in the Southeast Hotel in Nanjing. After investigation, it was reported to the police station, and both the person and the stolen goods were seized and sent to the Jiangning District Court for handling. It was not that we refused and falsely accused her. The newspaper had words such as "working together to drive out Jiazhen, accusing her of adultery," which is error four. As for our son Xiu Qian, he has been ruled by the Jiangning Court as the heir to the late husband's estate. Wang Jiazhen, due to adultery, has lost her status as a family member and has no right to claim alimony, according to the Supreme Court's interpretation and the precedent of the Dali Court. The opinion letter submitted by Lawyer Zhang Shizhao in this case is divided into four points, leaving people in a fog. Lawyer Zhang is simultaneously acting as the agent for the plaintiff, Wang Jiazhen, requesting 42,000 yuan in alimony, advocating starting from protecting the estate, detaining the proposed 120,000 yuan, and hoping that gentry in Guizhou who have connections would come forward to manage it. Since we have a biological son, the estate belongs to the son and is inherited according to law, which has already been ruled by the court. It is not a comparable situation with an ownerless estate, so what is there to protect and manage? Furthermore, demanding a huge amount of alimony from the late husband's biological son and virtuous wife by a runaway adulteress, and attempting to damage the estate by recklessly requesting detention, there is no legal precedent to allow it. We previously hired your esteemed lawyer as a year-round legal counsel, responsible for safeguarding reputation and other legal rights, which has been advertised in newspapers such as Shen Xin Times. Now that the report damages our reputation, we should request a representative to send a letter to the editor of Shen Bao, requesting that this letter be published in the newspaper's correspondence column or other equivalent position, in place of a correction, to avoid confusion. This would be greatly appreciated. After verifying the mentioned points, they are all consistent with the case file evidence and legal precedents. We hereby request your newspaper to verify and publish this, correct the factual errors, and protect the reputation of the parties involved. This is greatly appreciated. Respectfully addressed to the editor of Shen Bao, Lawyer Shan Yuhua, April 29th. I hereby state that yesterday, on May 5th, I read in your newspaper that Yang Xianbang came to our hospital for treatment, and that Tao Shuzhen was taking care of him, etc. Reading this was very surprising because our hospital is a maternity and child care hospital. How could Yang Xianbang come to our hospital for treatment? Since the opening of our hospital, there has also been no one named Tao Shuzhen. How could this have happened? Because it is related to the reputation of our hospital, please make a correction on our behalf. This is respectfully addressed to the editor, Bethel Hospital, respectfully. Educational News.

Exhaustion of Jiangsu Provincial Education Funds 146

▲ Schools will distribute income on a pro rata discounted basis upon opening. ▲ Grades 1, 2, and 3 may not be paid according to the budget. | Only 2,612,000 yuan collected this year | | Education Funds Management Office returns to Funds Committee | The Jiangsu Education Funds Management Office sent a letter to the Jiangsu Education Funds Committee, stating: In response to your committee's letter No. 31, approving the six proposals sent by principals of Jiangsu Provincial Secondary Schools, such as Wang Maozu, to be submitted for discussion at the 29th meeting, its sixth proposal requests that the Management Office be responsible for handling the disbursement of funds for this year in accordance with the following three items: (1) The disbursement of January funds should be completed by the end of April at the latest; (2) The notification of the allocation of February funds to counties should be issued by the end of April at the latest; (3) The disbursement of March funds should be completed by June 20th at the latest. This was resolved at the 29th meeting of this committee to be communicated to the Management Office for disbursement as requested. Accordingly, an excerpt of the proposal is sent for your information and disbursement, etc. Upon approval, it was found that last year's floods caused severe damage. Director Chen Mengzhao of the Finance Department, knowing that the special education funds for the 20th year would be greatly affected, also inquired and accurately estimated the collectible amount. It was roughly estimated that the salt, teeth, and land taxes would amount to 2.35 million yuan, which was communicated to your committee for verification, and relief was requested. At that time, it was only the flood. The foreign invasion had not yet spread to Jiangsu Province. By this year, the Japanese military had provoked incidents, occupied Shanghai and Zhejiang, and wars continued. Director Zhou Fohai knew that tax collection would be even more difficult. On February 15th, your committee convened the 28th meeting and proposed to formulate measures for the reduction of expenses for provincial educational institutions during the national crisis, in order to economize and maintain the situation. It was jointly resolved that the expenses of provincial educational institutions from December of the 20th year must be maintained according to the budget. The Management Office should do its best to raise funds. If there is a shortfall, the primary school funds, boarding fees for normal school students, and overseas study funds should be disbursed according to the original amount on a monthly basis. In addition, schools in the war zone that cannot open should be given maintenance fees at their discretion, and the rest should be distributed on a pro rata discounted basis. When the situation stabilizes, income increases, and disbursement can be made according to the original amount, the discounted amount should be stopped and the previously discounted amount should be compensated, etc. This is also a temporary measure to maintain the situation by adjusting expenditures to income. This office is preparing to allocate funds accordingly. Now that the previous reason is approved, the budget is still required to be disbursed according to the budget during the national crisis, which seems to conflict with the 28th resolution. According to the various incomes of this year, as of now, there are more than 2,158,000 yuan, plus more than 454,000 yuan of funds allocated to counties, totaling more than 2,612,000 yuan. (The financial department's subsidy has not been received.) Based on the estimated amount, it has already been exceeded, and resources have been exhausted. Now, there is a deadline for disbursing the funds for the first three months of the year to various schools, totaling more than 936,000 yuan, which is difficult to raise in a prosperous year and a peaceful time. At this time of famine and war, Jiangbei is affected by floods, and Jiangnan is also affected by military affairs. Tax revenue is insufficient, and there is little money to be transferred. Even the funds allocated by various counties have not been paid in full. Where can a large amount of income come from? In addition, financial stagnation and banks' refusal to lend make it impossible to accommodate. Resources are exhausted, and there is nothing to pay. This is due to natural disasters and man-made disasters, and there is nothing that can be done. However, schools are in difficulty and should do their best to maintain this. It is already impossible to find a way. What about the funds for the fourth, fifth, and sixth months? Accordingly, we request your committee to deliberate and provide guidance so that we can follow it. We are extremely anxious to await your instructions. Respectfully addressed to the Jiangsu Education Funds Committee.

End of Student Unrest at Xuzhou Middle School in Jiangsu Province 148

▲ Students have already left the school. The student unrest at Xuzhou Middle School in Jiangsu Province, caused by the issue of visiting the Third Normal School, has been reported in this newspaper several times. It is now learned that Inspector Yi had no choice but to consult with the school authorities to temporarily suspend meals, and at the same time notify the students' parents to take back the troublemaking students, and issue each person a travel allowance of ten yuan. Except for the students in the third year of general studies who had declared to the school that they had not joined, and left the school as a whole on the 5th, the remaining students expressed to Inspector Yi after several meetings that they were also willing to leave the school. On the morning of the 7th, all the high school students had collected their money and left the school. The unrest seems to have come to an end. Junior high school classes may be resumed recently. Boy Scouts Gradually Return to Shanghai from the Front Lines 149

Since the Shanghai Incident, the Shanghai Municipal Council of the Boy Scouts of China has organized a battlefield service team, dividing it into two offices: the military office and the rear office, to direct the work of the team members. It has been more than three months since then. It is now learned that the military office, due to the signing of the Shanghai Armistice Agreement, the end of the war, and the conclusion of the work, the more than 150 Boy Scouts working on the front lines are now being withdrawn. In addition to the more than 80 people who have returned to Shanghai, there are still more than 40 people in the engineering team building the city in Suzhou, and more than 30 people in the communication team at the Zhengyi headquarters of the Kunshan Transportation Department. As the work has not been completed, it is expected that all of them will return to Shanghai before the 15th of the month.
