Shanghai's Educational Undertakings After January 28th (1) Shang 152

▲ Schools closed due to the outbreak of war. ▲ Staff and students died in accidents. The left-wing writer Sinclair in New Continent published the following passage at the beginning of his book criticizing American education ("The Goose-Step"): "Today, millions of young people are studying in schools. They are the lifeline of our nation and the cornerstone of our country's future. If they receive a sound education, the country will be peaceful and great. Otherwise, there is little hope for everything." Indeed, education is the most fundamental undertaking for saving and building the country, which no one can deny. The country's poverty is not true poverty, but the lack of knowledge of young children is true poverty. The Japanese's strong armor and cannons sank Wusong Zhabei. Shanghai will never go bankrupt, but the destruction of cultural institutions in Wusong Zhabei means Shanghai will truly go bankrupt. The Japanese army seems to have clearly seen this. After the outbreak of the January 28th Shanghai Incident, wherever the enemy's footprints reached, schools, libraries, and bookstores were all ravaged. This loss cannot be redeemed by anything. Let us wipe away our tears, endure the pain, and calculate the account for Shanghai's education sector after January 28th.

1. Population Casualties 153

The school calendar for the 20th year stipulates that February 1st is the beginning of the second semester. As the day approached for schools at all levels to start classes, the January 28th Shanghai Incident occurred. Some schools, enthusiastic about education and serious about running schools, planned to make up for the students' missed studies in the previous semester due to the fall of the Northeast by starting school early. Therefore, most of the school's faculty and staff went to school, and students entered school together. They were preparing to spend a peaceful teaching and studying life of ringing bells for class and shaking bells after class. Unexpectedly, the enemy's guns and cannons and bombs awakened their good dreams, and they could not even attend the (last lesson). Even if they had heard the news beforehand that the situation was tight, the intelligent intellectual class would naturally join the masses and move away like ants. However, after all, many people learned from the government's (calm) attitude and did nothing. As a result, the male and female teachers and students of Guangdong primary and secondary schools were displaced, and the whereabouts of the principal of Chongde Girls' Middle School had to be inquired about by the administrative organs. Li Shicen of the Commercial Press escaped danger by claiming illness, and Shen Baiying carried the burden of young refugees and fled. 1,473 pieces of luggage from Shanghai Law School disappeared. Everyone was concerned about their own lives, who would care about the education undertaking that is the foundation of the country? Cautious people, learning from the ancient saying "evacuate to the city in minor unrest and evacuate to the countryside in major unrest," abandoned Shanghai, which was usually the focus of attention, and sang the song of returning home and retreating to the inland. However, what about the staff and students who returned to their hometown but could not see their parents? They can only wander like stateless White Russians, or be slaughtered like chickens, ducks, pigs, and sheep. The reporter paid attention to the reports in the newspapers or the reports of friends, and investigated the casualties of the population of schools at all levels in 137 schools in the war zone. The circumstances are described as follows: Student Zhou of Soochow University, Yao Jingfei of Chih Tze University, Zhao Bishi, director of academic affairs of Soochow Second Middle School, Li Boyi, director of the dormitory of Guangzhao Primary School, and his two sons, Jiang Da, a school worker at Southeast Medical College, Yang Ada, a school worker at Chih Tze Affiliated Middle School, Wang, a maidservant, Pan Aq, a gatekeeper at Guangdong Primary School, Tao Ada, a school worker, and others all died in accidents. Four students from Great China University (it is said that two students have been released by the Japanese command), Tan Bian, a technician at the Jiaotong University factory (living in Dade Lane, North Sichuan Road), Yang Xianwen, Yang Boren, Chen Dehua, students of Jinan University, Wang Yongzhen, a student of Nanyang High School of Commerce, Zhang Qihou, a teacher at Sanyu Primary School, Jiang Shixu, a teacher at Qingbai Primary School, and his family of six, Jiang Shengzhi, a teacher, Zhang Gensong and Zhang Yagen of the German Poultry School, Fang Xuejian, an employee of the White Goose Painting Tutoring School, etc., are still missing. Chen Huadong, a student at the Land Hospital of Zhongda Medical College, Chen Shidao, an employee of the Art College, Feng Hepu, Feng Kanglan, and Miss Ma, a Western teacher at Chongde Girls' Middle School, Wu Jingshan, an employee of Nanyang High School of Commerce, etc., were injured. There are also many school workers who were injured or missing. What kind of reaction do readers have to this ominous news besides sighing and complaining?

Significant Increase in Cotton Yarn Sales 158

The cotton yarn market has seen significant progress, showing a vibrant atmosphere. Genuine needs among customers have greatly increased. The enthusiasm of buyers from all sides marks the first surge since the Shanghai Incident. This is mainly due to the signing of the Sino-Japanese ceasefire agreement, the withdrawal of Japanese troops, and the gradual restoration of transportation. In terms of financial resources, the financial sector has been able to adjust and assist, unlike the sluggishness of previous days. As a result, people's spirits have been lifted. Additionally, the price of 20-count "Ren Zhong" yarn is 23 taels lower than the peak in February. Given the slightly improved environment, various customers have been actively procuring, leading to a sudden and prosperous turnaround in the long-depressed yarn sales. However, Japanese factories have fully resumed operations, making great efforts in production. Regarding sales, they are proceeding vigorously. Therefore, the best Chinese yarn does not need to be discounted, but should follow the trend and clear out the bottom stock. Future prospects will still depend on the current situation. It is observed that the Guangdong customers have made the most purchases. Due to the suspension of bidding for "Biao" yarn on the 59th, the reopening of bidding tomorrow is expected to bring a rise of one or two taels, as the current increase in genuine demand may excite people's spirits. Total daily purchases of spot yarn by various customers are estimated at 2,500 bales. Market prices have risen by 2.5 to 5 qian. Most of the Spring Silkworms in Zhuji Turned Yellow 162

▲ Terrible Weather... No Hope for Silk Harvest

In recent years, the silk industry in Zhuji, Zhejiang, has been developing rapidly. Last year, due to damage from the weather, the silk harvest was greatly reduced. This year, farmers fear repeating the same mistake as last spring. Furthermore, the rural economy is strained. The number of silkworm eggs raised is only about 40% of last year's. After the silkworms hatched, there were continuous cloudy and rainy days, and the climate temperature was not high, which was unfavorable for development. Until the middle of the third molt, the leaves were abundant. After a stuffy and hot day and night, 30-40% of the silkworms were lost. The early silkworms have already entered the major molt. Unexpectedly, the weather suddenly turned strangely cold again, and it was cloudy and rainy with no sunshine. The silkworms all suffered from insomnia and stopped eating. This year's silk harvest will be hopeless again.

Britain and Canada Impose Import Taxes on Chinese Tea 165

The British government previously proposed to increase the import tax on Chinese tea by 50%. According to news from London yesterday, this proposal has been implemented since the 1st of this month. The method is to add 4 pence for each pound of tea. According to the current shilling calculation, it is equivalent to 25 taels of Chinese silver per dan. Combining with the previous tax rate, each dan needs to be taxed 50 taels of Chinese silver. However, the British government has not discussed adding taxes on the import of red tea from Indian territories. According to general tea industry experts, the purpose of the British government's heavy taxation of Chinese tea is to curb the development of Chinese tea trade with Britain and to promote the prosperity of territorial tea industry.

Qimen and Fuliang Tea Firms Open Scales Together 166

Yesterday (30th), the various routes of Qimen and Fuliang autumn red tea, due to the sunny and warm weather, mountain households took advantage of the situation to dry the tea leaves and rushed to pick, rub, and make tea, and the shipments were very abundant. The main branch firms all opened scales together today to compete for procurement. The market price opened in the Baimao Port area of Fuliang at 90 yuan per dan, and the price in the Hantan area was 70 yuan, which was 7-8 yuan higher than the old price. The price in the Xianglin Bay and Yingxi areas of Qiu opened at 70-90 yuan, which was also 10 yuan higher than last year. The price in the southwest of Qimen still opened at around 100 yuan, which was no increase or decrease from the previous market price. If the weather is sunny and without rain for several days, the new tea can be collected together. Currently, each firm is trapped by insufficient cash and cannot buy as much as possible, which is a great regret.

Therefore, mountain households, due to the strong demand from the tea firms and in order to make profit off high prices, plan to give priority to picking and making tea leaves from Zhouyuan in the next few days to meet the demand.

Wuyuan Head Tea Begins to Be Picked and Made 168

In previous years, the new tea from various villages in Wuyuan County usually opened gardens before the Beginning of Summer. This year, due to the cold weather after Qingming, the development of tea buds was slow, and mountain tea only showed silver tips. In the past two days, the weather suddenly turned warm, and the rain stopped, and the tea trees quickly became green and lush. As the Beginning of Summer is approaching, the mountain households are deeply concerned that they will not be able to pick and make the tea in time, and those households with a lack of labor, and early tea in the northeast, have already begun to pick and hurry to pick on the 2nd (today), while the remaining mountain households in various villages are currently busy preparing firewood, rice, and miscellaneous items in preparation for entering the market within the next few days.

Xiushui Red Tea Market Momentum is Sluggish 169

Xiushui, Wuning, and Tonggu counties in Jiangxi have long been important producing areas of red tea. In recent years, due to soil deterioration and the lack of management by mountain households, the quality and taste have deteriorated. The sales of red tea from the counties of Xiushui and Wuning in Shanghai foreign firms have become increasingly narrow. Last year, 50-60 firms in the Xiushui and Wuning counties relied on Shanghai warehouses to enter the mountains to remit money and barely opened the market. The tea produced in boxes totaled around 20,000 boxes. This year, the red flames in the Xiushui and Tonggu counties are still high. Foreign tea firms are all afraid and dare not open the market. None of the Shanghai tea warehouses enter the mountains to welcome guests. The economy of local firms is even more difficult as a result. Except for tea firms with more abundant capital from enemy families, who have already planned to leave the village and open the scales, the rest are watching and not moving forward. The market momentum is extremely sluggish.

Free Talk

Miscellaneous Records of Japan (Part 1) 177

— Ou Xin

I have been doing business in Japan for many years. Since the September 18th Incident last year, overseas Chinese have been increasingly discriminated against. Two months ago, my store's associate, Mr. Liu, was killed, and the store was also destroyed. I had no choice but to close down and return to my country. Before leaving Japan, I traveled to various parts of Tokyo to observe and learn. I saw and heard a lot. I will select a few to tell the people of our country. Recently, Tokyo has been filled with the clouds of war. The Japanese military department claims that the war between Japan and the United States is not far away. It has ordered all troops to be armed and prepared, and is engaged in the construction of defense projects. The Navy has secretly deployed torpedoes in key fortresses. Anti-aircraft equipment has also been prepared. It is now actively building underground railways and military factories. The Japanese government is also planning to move the capital to Korea. A portion has already been secretly moved. The plan is that if it is to fight the United States alone, it will strike first, take the Philippines directly, and eliminate the US Far East Fleet. Then it will attack San Francisco. If Britain and the United States join forces, it will take a defensive position, with the Navy fully defending Tokyo, abandoning Taiwan. If it wins, it will capture Singapore and the Philippines. If it loses, it will withdraw from the mainland and defend Korea and the northeastern part of China. The Japanese suffered heavy losses in this Shanghai War. The total number of soldiers killed and wounded was about 23,000. In particular, the naval landing force suffered even more casualties on January 28th and 29th. Almost none of the 3,000 men survived. Admiral Osumi was deeply saddened by the news. He once wept and said to others: "The Empire has been training the Navy for 30 years, and it has always been praised by countries around the world. Now it has been beaten so badly by the Chinese army. If we encounter a powerful enemy in the future, it will be even more unimaginable."

A Calamitous Wedding Day 178

— Yi Qiu

Several days before our army retreated to the second line of defense, the Japanese army used aircraft to reconnoiter and drop bombs between Suzhou, Changzhou, Kunshan, and Taicang. Our people have suffered countless disasters. Mr. Xu Delin, a new employee of the county party headquarters in this county, told me about a tragedy after escaping from Luodian. So far, I have searched the newspapers in Suzhou and Shanghai, but there is no record of this. Therefore, I am urgently recording it to prove the brutality of the Japanese. When the Japanese army fiercely attacked Liuhe, the area around Luodian was often patrolled by Japanese aircraft. The villagers had become accustomed to it. Therefore, all the celebrations with relatives and friends were as usual. One day, in a village about two miles northeast of Luodian, a villager named Zhang was marrying a daughter-in-law for his son. He still followed the old-fashioned wedding ceremony. The auspicious time had arrived, and firecrackers were set off. At that time, a Japanese aircraft flew near the area. Suddenly, a crackling sound was heard. Assuming it was the firing of our army, they fled in a hurry. After a while, the sound of grinding in the sky became louder. A large number of bombers flew over and dropped bombs one after another. The villagers did not pay attention to it at first. At this point, they began to panic and tell each other. But the bombs had already fallen like rain, and flames were raging. They were unable to avoid and were buried in the fire. Before long, the entire village was destroyed. The dead were lying everywhere. The Japanese aircraft then soared away. Alas, the villagers were innocent and suffered this calamity. It was truly tragic.

World Anecdotes 179

— Hai Ke

Walking fish can only use their tails to swim in the water. This is known to everyone. In the eyes of ordinary people, when fish swim in the water, it seems that they rely on their caudal fins. The faster the caudal fin moves, the faster it swims. The muscles on both sides of the fish's body then allow it to swim freely in the water. However, after various tests, it is now known that fish can not only swim, but some fish can even come out of the water to climb trees or walk. Recently, many walking fish arrived at the London Zoo. They came from Java. When they come out of the water, they can use their pectoral fins as legs and feet to walk on the ground. There is also a kind of fish that can live outside the water for several days and can climb tall palm trees. The ancients said "(climbing trees to catch fish)" has really come true.

Grinding the Sword

Huang Chuang (Part 1) 180

— ·Gu· Ming·Dao

At the end of the Ming Dynasty, Shi Kefa supervised the army in Yangzhou, planning to recover lost territory. He used the Four Towns as a shield. The main generals of the Four Towns were Gao Jie, Huang Degong, Liu Zeqing, and Liu Liangzuo, all brave men. Among them, Gao Jie was the most tyrannical, and Huang Degong was the most valiant. It is a pity that they suspected each other and did not cooperate with each other, so they were defeated and destroyed by the Qing army. When Huang Degong first started out, he walked on foot as a whip-wielding servant for merchants. When he entered the capital via Shandong, he encountered bandits. The merchants all fled, but Degong alone held two donkey hooves to defend against the bandits. He was invincible and killed more than ten people. People were all surprised by this. Later, he made meritorious service in Hebei and was named Earl of Jingnan. He once defeated Zhang Xianzhong's roving bandits at Fangling in Qianshan, killing ten thousand of them. Zhang Xianzhong was almost captured. Degong was honest and loyal. Although his troops were not many, he always charged ahead in battle, as swift as a flash. The people of Jianghuai were amazed and called him invincible, calling him Huang Chuang. Among the roving bandits, there was a young and brave general called the Invincible General, who was the only one who did not submit. When he met Degong, he said to his comrades: "Why are you so timid? I will capture Huang Degong for you." The bandits all watched with bated breath. The Invincible General took a long knife and charged into battle, shouting with glaring eyes. He rushed to Degong. Degong brandished a golden mace and rode his horse to meet him. He immediately captured him, placed him horizontally on the horse, held down his shoulder with his left hand, and galloped away with his right hand whipping the horse. The bandits were demoralized and warned each other: "You must avoid Huang Chuang." His courage was like this. At this time of urgent foreign aggression, when we hear the drums and think of generals, brave warriors can revive the country. ▲ Correction: Yesterday's article was the second part. It should be switched with today's first part.

Record of Military Life in Double Buildings (47) 181

— Master of Seeking Happiness Studio

Chapter 6: Pitiable Night of Sharing Dreams, Forced into an Alliance Under the Bed, Still Remembers the Time of First Love, Betrays the Promise by the Window. An Yutian had a fellow-township relationship with her. He had met her in the assembly hall of the Beijing Students' Association of Fellow Townsmen early on, but they had not had any deep friendship. The reason why their two hearts suddenly came together was due to the medium of that whatchamacallit April 27th student movement. On that day, April 27th of the previous year, students from various national schools in Beijing, for some particularly major issue, suddenly launched a most violent student movement, gathering thousands and thousands of male and female students, marching in columns, flying various colored flags, shouting various slogans, distributing various leaflets, and heading mightily, like angry waves, to the location of government agencies to make some request. In fact, the request did not seem to be such a terribly scary thing. It was only laughable that those big figures in power were too timid. Upon receiving such a bizarre report, they stubbornly claimed that the students were going to come to kill and set fires. They were so scared that they were covered in excrement and urine. They didn't even care about opening any kind of national conference. They hurriedly ran away through the back door, disappearing without a trace. Someone, I don't know which high-minded big shot, having escaped to an extremely safe place, a room in a hotel in Dongjiaominxiang, somewhat calmed his frightened soul, and suddenly thought of issuing orders, deploying troops and defenses to preserve that big government office, lest it be truly destroyed by the students, so that officials could rely on the temple to receive incense forever. These several phone calls were made, and immediately countless teams of soldiers and police were transferred to the front of that government gate. Swords were drawn, bows were strung, guns were in hand, and cannons were arranged like a forest, surrounding the big government office layer upon layer like an iron barrel. Like facing a major enemy, they waited for the students to come and kill. Moving on, those many male and female students did come, shouting earth-shattering slogans, and the several representatives at the front, holding a petition like a doctoral dissertation, were about to step forward to submit the letter. However, they were blocked by the four iron-barred gates that were tightly closed. Immediately, they shook the iron bars and loudly negotiated a few words, but still no one came out to answer. Only a row of soldiers and police inside could be seen glaring at the students, their teeth gnashing, wanting to shout the students back. Thus, the students shouted outside, and the soldiers and police roared inside. Just as they were deadlocked, several small stones, no one knew where they came from, flew into the gate. The soldiers and police immediately obeyed the order to not start trouble first and to maintain order, thinking that they had an opportunity to act.

Shanghai Shenbao Local Supplement 182

Speech

The Longevity Character in Wu Xiucai's Hall 183

— Jin

Yesterday's newspaper reported that Wu Peifu's residence in Beiping has a longevity character written by a spirit medium hanging high in the hall. It is inscribed "Written by Qingxuan Elder, bestowed upon Zhixuan." Zhixuan is Wu Xiucai's religious name. I will not criticize Wu Xiucai's talent and character for now. However, Wu Xiucai can be said to be a superstitious person. Today, I will use Xiucai as an example to raise the issue of superstition and discuss it. In the end... what are the crimes of superstition? What are the benefits of not being superstitious? The slogan of eradicating superstition has long been shouted to the skies. In recent years, it has become even more vigorous. A few years ago, the city gods and earth gods suffered great misfortune, some were placed in cold palaces, and some were thrown into the Eastern Seas. Most pitifully, those fortune tellers who analyze characters, cast lots, and are blind were forced to change their professions. May I ask, in today's China, where livelihoods are declining, even highly educated university graduates or foreign-educated doctors and masters cannot find jobs for the time being. What profession can you ask a few blind gentlemen to change to? This is one example. Recently, in the battles in Wusong and Zhabei, countless amulets with the image of "Namo Amitabha" were found on the bodies of Japanese soldiers. The other day, they held a memorial service for the fallen soldiers and invited many Japanese monks to deliver the souls of foreign ghosts. Judging from this, the degree of superstition in Japan is not less than in our country, but their culture is still progressing, and their national strength is still expanding. It can be seen that superstition does not necessarily hinder culture, and it does not necessarily hinder the development of the country. On the other hand, not being superstitious has not been seen to have any benefits. This is another example. Indeed, I cannot say that their evolution is due to superstition, but I can also say that superstition has nothing to do with evolution. Our country's poor politics and backward culture are not improved through effort, but we are eagerly abandoning the fundamental for the superficial, and only making the eradication of superstition our task. As a result, we only lost the faith of ordinary men and women and increased the number of unemployed in an already boring life. What benefit is there in asking? If we go further, not to mention the extremely barbaric nations, even in European and American countries, how strong and widespread is the religious thought of their people? Is it not also superstition? In the end, it has not deprived them of the title of civilized countries, nor has it blocked their path to national strength. If we say it more broadly, everyone has some superstitious color. Since it is called superstition, there must be an object of superstition. The object does not necessarily have to be gods, demons, and ghosts to be considered superstition. Those who are enthusiastic about wealth and status take promotion and wealth as their object; those who are addicted to lust take modern girls as their object; those who like to drink old wine take Shaoxing sorghum as their object; those who have a hibiscus addiction take Chen Gong ointment as their object; those who are addicted to gambling take XX Company XX Association as their object; fashionable girls and frivolous young men take dance halls and movie theaters as their object; those who boast of extravagance take Western-style houses, cars, and the strange and beautiful clothes and luxurious items displayed in the three companies as their object. Can these objects not also be said to be superstition? If we ask a judge to judge the crimes of the above two types of superstition, I think the former is only a slight crime of negligence, while the latter is a crime of "public danger". Note: The crime of public danger is by no means explained in this way in law, but only a term is borrowed for application.

### Miscellaneous Poems on Current Events 185

— Bao Ren

The east wind blows rain again, Qingming, the Hu cavalry enter the Han city one after another. No wonder the brave troops number ten thousand, but they use peace talks to answer the rise of peace. The cannon rumbles, and the warships are tall, the banners and streamers embrace the sea, the rear army has no succession, losing the previous battle, sadly listening to the river wind roaring with angry waves. The sound of the machines rumbles, shaking the earth, looking back at Wusong with lingering sorrow, the coastal plants are mostly remnants, tears sprinkled on the riverbank to talk about the ashes of the disaster. The battle blood is still fishy, and the bones are not yet cold, enduring the humiliation to talk about sorrows and joys, who can save the sand worms and apes, the picturesque rivers and mountains are unbearable to look at.

Science

Homemade Soda and Its Principles 186

— Ke

The weather is getting hotter day by day, and soda (according to the Western name AeratedWater, the original meaning should be carbonic acid water) is also gradually on the market, so I specially write out the method of making soda, and at the same time make a simple exploration of soda. (A) Materials: (1) Citric acid (CitricacidHC6H5O7) | This acid is mostly contained in fruits, containing one molecule of water, forming colorless crystals, easily soluble in water, and the acidity is very refreshing. (2) Baking soda (BicarbonateofSodaNaHCO3) | That is, sodium bicarbonate, commonly known as baking soda. The above two items are sold in pharmacies everywhere. (B) Preparation | Cold boiled water, soda bottles with marbles, fruit syrup, saccharin or sugar juice, other various spices such as banana oil, etc., a scale. (C) Method | First pour the fruit syrup, sugar juice, spices, etc. into the bottle, about one-quarter (using the bottle as a unit), then pour in cold boiled water, then use the scale to weigh one-tenth of baking soda, first pour it into the bottle, then press it tightly with your palm, wait for the citric acid to enter the bottle, then quickly cover the bottle mouth with your palm, and quickly turn the bottle upside down. The faster the better. Because citric acid immediately undergoes a chemical change when it encounters baking soda, producing a large amount of carbon dioxide. The marble in the bottle falls down by the force of the gas and adheres tightly to the rubber band at the bottle mouth. At this time, the soda can be considered complete. If you want to drink it, you only need to push down the marble, just like the ones sold on the market, it will produce a lot of gas. If it is done properly, the taste is no less than those sold on the market. (D) Principles and Functions | The principle of soda is that citric acid reacts with baking soda to produce carbon dioxide. Carbon dioxide does not want to dissolve in water, but because the bottle mouth is tightly plugged, it cannot run out, so it has to dissolve in the water. When the stopper is opened, a part of the carbon dioxide runs out, and at the same time the pressure on the water surface is reduced, so the water bubbles, like boiling. The function is to be cool and refreshing, can quench thirst, and help digestion. Carbon dioxide entering the lungs is certainly harmful, but entering the stomach is not harmful. In addition, I would like to state that the soda sold on the market is not made in this way, because this method is only suitable for making a small amount, so it is only suitable for use in households. As for the soda on the market, it is made by using high pressure to dissolve a large amount of carbon dioxide in water, but the purpose is nothing more than to dissolve carbon dioxide in water.

Western-Suited Youths 187

— Ying Dai

Among the pedestrians on Nanjing Road, if we make a statistic, then the Western-suited youths who come and go account for at least one or two tenths. This time when I returned to Songjiang, on the most prosperous Yue Temple Street, I encountered Western-suited youths, probably accounting for one or two percent. Then from Songjiang back to my hometown, that is a deserted market town, with a small population. In the past, you couldn't find a single Western-suited youth on the street, but now there are also two or three Western-suited youths, their leather shoes clattering, wandering in our town. The mentality of Chinese youths is that wearing a Western suit is so beautiful, which is nothing more than being impulsed by vanity. In today's society, a student of middle or higher status occasionally goes out for social occasions, and if he doesn't wear a Western suit, he will inevitably feel inferior among many Western-suited friends. Therefore, even friends who are so poor that they cannot pay tuition fees must prepare a Western suit. Especially when the waves of open male and female social interaction and free love are rising day by day, a young person who has reached the stage of seeking a spouse must go out to socialize. But in the social scene, if you don't wear a Western suit, you may not be able to win the favor of modern girls because you are not decent and not spirited. At the same time, they seem to gain a lot of face among their female companions when they have a Western-suited youth as a lover. Therefore, the recent preference of young people for Western suits can be regarded as a manifestation of vanity and the psychology of seeking love.

He Hao Yi

(Hu Lifu)'s Question 189

— Xi Wu

On a Sunday afternoon, when it was about to rain, the air in the room was very tense, making people feel very stuffy. Bored, I happened to flip through the anti-Japanese calendar on the wall. The content was lively anti-Japanese paintings, plus many celebrities' handwriting, which was shocking and indeed a good plan for anti-Japanese resistance. On page fourteen, it was titled with the big characters "Students are the soul of a country," and signed "Hu Lifu." Cough, is it him? No, this is the anti-Japanese (Hu Lifu). He is a celebrity, he is an intellectual, and he will never abandon anti-Japanese resistance to flatter Japan. I once read a statement by another (Hu Lifu) in the newspaper. How many Hu Lifus are there? If it's not him, who is it? Is there a third (Hu Lifu)? Doubts were winding around the strings of my heart!

A Corner of Society

Sketches of Shanghai Three 190

— Wu

||Catching Crickets Why is picking up cigarette butts called catching crickets? Even A San, who catches crickets, doesn't quite understand this himself. But he can be considered to fully understand what catching crickets is all about. Judging from A San's age, he is still as young as the young masters who go to elementary school in cars, but since last year, he had to start living independently. Among his little urchin companions, he learned to pick up cigarette butts, and this became his only way of life. Every day is the same, he has to take his small cloth bag to the road in the morning to make a living. Tram stops, movie theater entrances, and all lively places are his best places to wander. He crowds in the crowd, carefully and continuously searching for his only source of livelihood. Recently, this kind of life has not been easy to do. In addition to the original opium-smoking friends, those who do the same job have also added a lot of drifters from foreign countries. So sometimes they will suffer insults or beatings from them due to their older age for competing for a relatively large cigarette butt, and sometimes even bleed. However, long-term experience has given him many valuable lessons. For example, in places like Carter Road and Nicheng Bridge, although there are many cigarette butts, they are only left with a little bit, and the tobacco leaves are inferior. On the contrary, in the Bund, Great Road, and Jing'an Temple Road areas, almost all of the picked up cigarette butts are top-quality tobacco and a very long section. Good tobacco can be sold for a good price. Therefore, the working-class areas of Carter Road and other places are ultimately worthy of cursing. (× His mother! | Throw away a cigarette butt after smoking it to such a small point,...) When he could only pick up cigarette butts less than half an inch after several days of rain, he often cursed ruthlessly like this.

Dr. Huang has special expertise in bone setting, toxicology, tuberculosis, leprosy, difficult childbirth, and other departments.

Civil First Instance Judgment 258

Chou Biekesheng vs. Jiang Zhaotong for Loan Case 259

(Main Text) The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 60 yuan, and the litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

A Mugsheng vs. Wang Dongru and Others for Loan Case 260

(Main Text) The defendant Wang Dongru shall repay the plaintiff 100 yuan. If this is not fulfilled, the defendant Wang Yonghao shall be responsible for repayment. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant Wang Dongru.

Meng Tesheng vs. Gao Lanbao for Loan Case 261

(Main Text) The defendant Gao Lanbao shall repay the plaintiff 300 yuan. If this is not fulfilled, the defendant Xing Jinxiang shall be responsible for repayment. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant Gao Lanbao.

Zhong Dingchen vs. Chen Jiefu for Land Price Case 262

(Main Text) The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 1,600 yuan and interest at an annual rate of 5% from the date of the lawsuit until the end of enforcement. The plaintiff's remaining claims are rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

Gong Shengxiang vs. Zheng Axing for Breach of Contract Case 263

(Main Text) The defendant shall immediately demolish the construction on the plaintiff's adjacent right-of-way. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

Shenchang Foreign Firm vs. Xu Tingyu for Debt Case 264

(Main Text) The defendant shall repay the plaintiff US$1,268.89. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

A Mugsheng vs. Zhu Youfa and Others for Loan Case 265

(Main Text) The defendant Zhu Youfa shall repay the plaintiff 40 yuan. If this is not fulfilled, the defendant Qian Gen shall be responsible for repayment. The defendant Qian Fugen shall repay the plaintiff 20 yuan. If this is not fulfilled, the defendant Zhang Xiaodi shall be responsible for repayment. The defendant Qian Fugen shall repay the plaintiff 60 yuan. If this is not fulfilled, the defendant Huang Xiaomei shall be responsible for repayment. The plaintiff's remaining claims are rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant Qian Fugen for 8/13, the defendant Zhu Youfa for 4/13, and the plaintiff for 1/13.

Lun Sheng vs. Li Deji and Others for Loan Case 266

(Main Text) The defendant Li Deji shall repay the plaintiff 180 yuan. The defendants Li Deji, Li Wangshi, and Zhao Dezhao shall jointly repay the plaintiff 190 yuan. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant Li Deji for the 180 yuan portion, and by the defendants Li Deji, Li Wangshi, and Zhao Dezhao jointly for the remaining portion.

Fuxing Land Renting Agency Zhu Chengqian vs. Defendant Dazhong Securities Firm for Rent Arrears Case 267

(Main Text) The defendant Dazhong Securities Firm shall repay the plaintiff 540 taels of silver and 4.5 yuan for street cleaning fees. If this cannot be repaid, the owner of the defendant Baofeng Ruiji Firm shall be responsible for repayment, and it is confirmed that the plaintiff has a lien on the furniture left by the defendant Dazhong Securities Firm in the rented premises. The plaintiff's remaining claims and application for provisional execution are rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff for 1/10 and the defendant Dazhong Securities Firm for 9/10.

Li Wei Furen vs. Te Bu Lu Fule Shi and Others for Return of Furniture Case 268

(Main Text) The plaintiff's claim is rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff.

Dalun Real Estate Company vs. Huatai Pharmacy for Rent Arrears Case 269

(Main Text) The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 3,528 taels of rent. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

Airlys Renting Agency Pan Shidun vs. Mrs. Wilson for Rent Arrears Case 270

(Main Text) The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 600 taels of silver. The lease agreement between the defendant and the plaintiff shall be terminated, and it is confirmed that the plaintiff has a lien on the movable property left by the defendant in the premises. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

Tongwen Printing Ink Company Cheng Jingyi vs. Ximei Printing House for Debt Case 271

(Main Text) The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 110 yuan and statutory interest from November 15, 1931, until the end of enforcement. The defendant shall also repay the plaintiff 39.3 yuan and statutory interest from December 28, 1931, until the end of enforcement. The defendant shall also repay the plaintiff 34.98 yuan and statutory interest from January 20, 1932, until the end of enforcement. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. This case shall be enforced.

Public Notice for Service of Process 272

For the public notice of service of process, in the case of Qian Juxi vs. Qian Wangshi for cohabitation dispute, as the whereabouts of the defendant Qian Wangshi are unknown and the documents cannot be served, the plaintiff has requested public notice for service of process, which has been approved by a ruling, and lawyer Peng Qixiu has been appointed as the defendant's special agent. This court has now set 2:00 PM on May 30th in the seventh courtroom as the date for public hearing. The defendant's summons shall be served by public notice in accordance with the law. The defendant is hereby notified to submit a reply before the hearing date and to appear in court on time for the hearing without delay. This public notice is hereby given to the defendant Qian Wangshi for information. (May 9th)
